\subsection*{Beilinson-audit status updates (2026-04-17)}

\begin{itemize}
\item \verb|thm:tempered-stratum-contains-wp| (Vol~II): downgraded
\textsc{ProvedHere} $\to$ \textsc{Conjectured} by commit
\texttt{a5640de}. Reason: Gurarie 1993 + Flohr 1996 logarithmic
amplitudes exhibit unbounded Massey products despite finite Zhu,
refuting the Zhu-bounded-Massey shortcut.

\item \verb|prop:programme-climax-nontempered-emptiness| (Vol~II):
SCOPE-QUALIFIED to non-logarithmic standard landscape.

\item CY-C pentagon stratification (Vol~III commit
\texttt{cade61c}): healed from
$\kappa_{\mathrm{ch}}^{R_i}\in\{3,12,24\}$ to
$\rho^{R_i}\in\{3,12,24\}$ (generator-lattice rank).
$\kappa_{\mathrm{ch}}=0$ route-independent by Hodge supertrace.

\item Kummer-irregular prime labels $\{1423, 3067, 23, 43, 419\}$
(Vol~I commit \texttt{9668336}): RETRACTED. These appear in
$S_r$-numerators as Riccati-arithmetic characteristic primes, not
Kummer-arithmetic. Tier-3 emergence corrected to~$\{37, 691, 811\}$.

\item Super-Yangian complementarity: corrected from naive
$\kappa+\kappa^!=0$ to
$\kappa(Y(\mathfrak{sl}(m|n)))+\kappa(Y(\mathfrak{sl}(n|m))^!)=\max(m,n)$
at Sugawara-shifted dual level \emph{in the Berezinian
normalisation}; in the super-trace normalisation,
$\kappa^{\str}+\kappa^{\str,!}=0$. Both parametrise the same
complementarity datum via the central automorphism~$\sigma_{\sBer}$
(Lemma~\ref{lem:super-trace-berezinian-bridge}). At
$\mathfrak{psl}(2|2)$, Beisert~2007 gives \emph{three} central
elements in the AdS/CFT extension $\mathfrak{psl}(2|2)\oplus
\mathbb{C}^{3}$; the coincidence with $\max(2,2)=2$ comes from the
centre \emph{rank} in that extension, not the central-element
count.
\end{itemize}
